<a id="14436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14364" class="Function">denot-twoᶜ</a> <a id="14447" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14448" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14448" class="Bound">u</a><a id="14449" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a><a id="14452" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14454" class="Bound">w</a><a id="14455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14457" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10142" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-intro</a> <a id="14469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10142" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-intro</a> <a id="14478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10004" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-elim</a> <a id="14486" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="14491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9925" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="14495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14537" class="Function">lt1</a><a id="14498" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10004" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-elim</a> <a id="14508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="14513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9925" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="14517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14620" class="Function">lt2</a><a id="14520" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9925" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a><a id="14525" class="Symbol">)))</a>
  <a id="14531" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="14537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14537" class="Function">lt1</a> <a id="14541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14454" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="14549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="14551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14448" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="14553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14454" class="Bound">w</a>
        <a id="14573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14537" class="Function">lt1</a> <a id="14577" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4691" class="InductiveConstructor">ConjR2⊑</a> <a id="14587" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4839" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun⊑</a> <a id="14593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a> <a id="14599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a><a id="14604" class="Symbol">)</a>
     
        <a id="14620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14620" class="Function">lt2</a> <a id="14624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14448" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="14628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="14634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14448" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="14636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="14644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="14646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14454" class="Bound">w</a>
        <a id="14656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#14620" class="Function">lt2</a> <a id="14660" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4617" class="InductiveConstructor">ConjR1⊑</a> <a id="14671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4839" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun⊑</a> <a id="14677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a> <a id="14683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a><a id="14688" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Next we have a classic example of self application: `Δ = λx. (x x)`.
The input value for `x` needs to be a table, and it needs to have an
entry that maps a smaller version of itself, call it `v`, to some value
`w`. So the input value looks like `v ↦ w ⊔ v`. Of course, then the
output of `Δ` is `w`. The derivation is given below.  The first occurrences
of `x` evaluates to `v ↦ w`, the second occurrence of `x` evaluates to `v`,
and then the result of the application is `w`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Δ"></a><a id="15195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15195" class="Function">Δ</a> <a id="15197" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="15201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="15203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>
<a id="15205" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15195" class="Function">Δ</a> <a id="15207" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="15212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4999" class="Function Operator">#</a> <a id="15215" class="Number">0</a><a id="15216" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="15220" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4999" class="Function Operator">#</a> <a id="15223" class="Number">0</a><a id="15224" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="denot-Δ"></a><a id="15228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15228" class="Function">denot-Δ</a> <a id="15236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15238" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15240" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15241" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="15243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15243" class="Bound">w</a><a id="15244" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15246" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7471" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="15251" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="15253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15195" class="Function">Δ</a> <a id="15255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="15257" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15259" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15241" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="15261" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="15263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15243" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="15265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15241" class="Bound">v</a><a id="15268" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="15272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15243" class="Bound">w</a><a id="15273" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15228" class="Function">denot-Δ</a> <a id="15283" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10142" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-intro</a> <a id="15293" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10004" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-elim</a> <a id="15301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15302" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="15306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9925" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="15310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4617" class="InductiveConstructor">ConjR1⊑</a> <a id="15319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a><a id="15324" class="Symbol">))</a>
                          <a id="15353" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="15358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9925" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="15362" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4691" class="InductiveConstructor">ConjR2⊑</a> <a id="15371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a><a id="15376" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

One might worry whether this semantics can deal with diverging
programs.  The `⊥` value and the `⊥-intro` rule provide a way to handle
them. (The `⊥-intro` rule is also what enables β reduction on
non-terminating arguments.)  The classic `Ω` program is a particularly
simple program that diverges. It applies `Δ` to itself. The semantics
assigns to `Ω` the meaning `⊥`. There are several ways to derive this, we
shall start with one that makes use of the `⊔-intro` rule.  First,
`denot-Δ` tells us that `Δ` evaluates to `((⊥ ↦ ⊥) ⊔ ⊥) ↦ ⊥`
(choose `v₁ = v₂ = ⊥`).  Next, `Δ` also evaluates to `⊥ ↦ ⊥` by use of
`↦-intro` and `⊥-intro` and to `⊥` by `⊥-intro`. As we saw previously,
whenever we can show that a program evaluates to two values, we can apply
`⊔-intro` to join them together, so `Δ` evaluates to `(⊥ ↦ ⊥) ⊔ ⊥`. This
matches the input of the first occurrence of `Δ`, so we can conclude that
the result of the application is `⊥`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Ω"></a><a id="16347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16347" class="Function">Ω</a> <a id="16349" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="16353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="16355" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>
<a id="16357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16347" class="Function">Ω</a> <a id="16359" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15195" class="Function">Δ</a> <a id="16363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="16365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15195" class="Function">Δ</a>

<a id="denot-Ω"></a><a id="16368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16368" class="Function">denot-Ω</a> <a id="16376" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7471" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="16381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="16383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16347" class="Function">Ω</a> <a id="16385" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="16387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="16389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16368" class="Function">denot-Ω</a> <a id="16397" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10004" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-elim</a> <a id="16406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#15228" class="Function">denot-Δ</a> <a id="16414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10341" class="InductiveConstructor">⊔-intro</a> <a id="16423" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10142" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-intro</a> <a id="16432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10266" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥-intro</a><a id="16439" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10266" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥-intro</a><a id="16448" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

A shorter derivation of the same result is by just one use of the
`⊥-intro` rule.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="denot-Ω&#39;"></a><a id="16559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16559" class="Function">denot-Ω&#39;</a> <a id="16568" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7471" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="16573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="16575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16347" class="Function">Ω</a> <a id="16577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="16579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="16581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#16559" class="Function">denot-Ω&#39;</a> <a id="16590" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10266" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥-intro</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Just because one can derive `∅ ⊢ M ↓ ⊥` for some closed term `M` doesn't mean
that `M` necessarily diverges. There may be other derivations that
conclude with `M` producing some more informative value.  However, if
the only thing that a term evaluates to is `⊥`, then it indeed it
diverges.

An attentive reader may have noticed a disconnect earlier in the way
we planned to solve the self-application problem and the actual
`↦-elim` rule for application. We said at the beginning that we would
relax the notion of table lookup, allowing an argument to match an
input entry if the argument is equal or greater than the input entry.
Instead, the `↦-elim` rule seems to require an exact match.  However,
because of the `sub` rule, application really does allow larger
arguments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↦-elim2"></a><a id="17403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17403" class="Function">↦-elim2</a> <a id="17411" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17413" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="17415" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17416" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="17417" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17419" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17420" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="17422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="17428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17416" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="17429" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17431" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17432" class="Bound">M₁</a> <a id="17435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17435" class="Bound">M₂</a> <a id="17438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17438" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="17441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17441" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="17444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17444" class="Bound">v₃</a><a id="17446" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="17456" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17420" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="17460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="17462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17432" class="Bound">M₁</a> <a id="17465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="17467" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17438" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="17471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="17473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17444" class="Bound">v₃</a><a id="17475" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="17485" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17420" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="17489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="17491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17435" class="Bound">M₂</a> <a id="17494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="17496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17441" class="Bound">v₂</a>
        <a id="17507" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17438" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="17512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="17514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17441" class="Bound">v₂</a>
          <a id="17527" class="Comment">------------------</a>
        <a id="17554" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17420" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="17558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="17560" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17432" class="Bound">M₁</a> <a id="17564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="17566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17435" class="Bound">M₂</a><a id="17568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="17572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17444" class="Bound">v₃</a>
<a id="17575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17403" class="Function">↦-elim2</a> <a id="17583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17583" class="Bound">d₁</a> <a id="17586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17586" class="Bound">d₂</a> <a id="17589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17589" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="17592" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10004" class="InductiveConstructor">↦-elim</a> <a id="17601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17583" class="Bound">d₁</a> <a id="17604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="17609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17586" class="Bound">d₂</a> <a id="17612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17589" class="Bound">lt</a><a id="17614" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Denotations and denotational equality

Next we define a notion of denotational equality based on the above
semantics. Its statement makes use of an if-and-only-if, which we
define as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_iff_"></a><a id="17838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17838" class="Function Operator">_iff_</a> <a id="17844" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17846" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="17850" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17852" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="17856" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17858" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="17862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17862" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17864" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17838" class="Function Operator">iff</a> <a id="17868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17868" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="17870" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17872" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17862" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17875" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17868" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="17878" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17880" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="17882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17883" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17868" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="17885" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#17862" class="Bound">P</a><a id="17888" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Another way to view the denotational semantics is as a function that
maps a term to a relation from environments to values.  That is, the
_denotation_ of a term is a relation from environments to values.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Denotation"></a><a id="18120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18120" class="Function">Denotation</a> <a id="18131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="18141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18143" class="PrimitiveType">Set₁</a>
<a id="18148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18120" class="Function">Denotation</a> <a id="18159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18159" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18161" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="18168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18159" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18170" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="18178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18180" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18183" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The following function ℰ gives this alternative view of the semantics,
which really just amounts to changing the order of the parameters.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ℰ"></a><a id="18349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18349" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="18351" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18353" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="18355" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18355" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18356" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18358" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18361" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="18363" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18355" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="18369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="18370" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18372" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18120" class="Function">Denotation</a> <a id="18385" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18355" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="18387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18349" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="18389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18389" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="18391" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18393" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18395" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="18397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18397" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="18399" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18395" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="18403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="18405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18389" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="18407" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="18409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18397" class="Bound">v</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In general, two denotations are equal when they produce the same
values in the same environment.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18534" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="18540" class="Number">3</a> <a id="18542" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18547" class="Function Operator">_≃_</a>

<a id="18599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18547" class="Function Operator">_≃_</a> <a id="18604" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18605" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18606" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18608" href="{% class="Function">Env</a> <a id="18626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18605" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18627" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18629" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18608" class="Bound">D₁</a> <a id="18648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18632" class="Bound">v</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Denotational equality is an equivalence relation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="≃-refl"></a><a id="18739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18739" class="Function">≃-refl</a> <a id="18746" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18748" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18750" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18751" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a><a id="18762" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18764" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18766" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18767" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="18769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18120" class="Function">Denotation</a> <a id="18782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#18751" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18783" class="Symbol">}</a>

out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19086" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="19131" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19088" class="Bound">v</a><a id="19132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19134" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19097" class="Bound">z</a><a id="19135" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19138" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a>
                        <a id="19164" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="19167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19167" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="19169" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19171" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#167" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="19177" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19078" class="Bound">eq1</a> <a id="19182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19086" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="19184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19088" class="Bound">v</a><a id="19185" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19187" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19188" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#167" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="19194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19082" class="Bound">eq2</a> <a id="19199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19086" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="19201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19088" class="Bound">v</a><a id="19202" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19204" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19167" class="Bound">z</a><a id="19205" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19208" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Two terms `M` and `N` are denotational equal when their denotations are
equal, that is, `ℰ M ≃ ℰ N`.

The following submodule introduces equational reasoning for the `≃`
relation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="19416" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="≃-Reasoning"></a><a id="19423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19423" class="Module">≃-Reasoning</a> <a id="19435" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19436" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19438" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19440" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a><a id="19447" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19449" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Road map for the following chapters

The subsequent chapters prove that the denotational semantics has
several desirable properties. First, we prove that the semantics is
compositional, i.e., that the denotation of a term is a function of
the denotations of its subterms. To do this we shall prove equations
of the following shape.

    ℰ (ƛ M) ≃ ... ℰ M ...
    ℰ (M · N) ≃ ... ℰ M ... ℰ N ...

The compositionality property is not trivial because the semantics we
have defined includes three rules that are not syntax directed:
`⊥-intro`, `⊔-intro`, and `sub`.

Next we investigate whether the denotational semantics and the
reduction semantics are equivalent. Recall that the job of a language
semantics is to describe the observable behavior of a given program
`M`. For the lambda calculus there are several choices that one can
make, but they usually boil down to a single bit of information:

  * divergence: the program `M` executes forever.
  * termination: the program `M` halts.

We can characterize divergence and termination in terms of reduction.

  * divergence: `¬ (M —↠ ƛ N)` for any term `N`.
  * termination: `M —↠ ƛ N` for some term `N`.

We can also characterize divergence and termination using denotations.

  * divergence: `¬ (∅ ⊢ M ↓ v ↦ w)` for any `v` and `w`.
  * termination: `∅ ⊢ M ↓ v ↦ w` for some `v` and `w`.

Alternatively, we can use the denotation function `ℰ`. 

  * divergence: `¬ (ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N))` for any term `N`.
  * termination: `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` for some term `N`.

So the question is whether the reduction semantics and denotational
semantics are equivalent.

    (∃ N. M —↠ ƛ N)  iff  (∃ N. ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N))

We address each direction of the equivalence in the second and third
chapters. In the second chapter we prove that reduction to a lambda
abstraction implies denotational equality to a lambda
abstraction. This property is called the _soundness_ in the
literature.

    M —↠ ƛ N  implies  ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)

In the third chapter we prove that denotational equality to a lambda
abstraction implies reduction to a lambda abstraction. This property
is called _adequacy_ in the literature.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

The proofs of these properties rely on some basic results about the
denotational semantics, which we establish in the rest of this
chapter.  We start with some lemmas about renaming, which are quite
similar to the renaming lemmas that we have seen in previous chapters.
We conclude with a proof of an important inversion lemma for the
less-than relation regarding function values.


## Renaming preserves denotations

We shall prove that renaming variables, and changing the environment
accordingly, preserves the meaning of a term. We generalize the
renaming lemma to allow the values in the new environment to be the
same or larger than the original values. This generalization is useful
in proving that reduction implies denotational equality.

As before, we need an extension lemma to handle the case where we
proceed underneath a lambda abstraction. Here, the nth function
performs lookup in the environment, analogous to `Γ ∋ A`.  Now suppose
that `ρ` is a renaming that maps variables in `γ` into variables with
equal or larger values in `δ`. This lemmas says that extending the
renaming producing a renaming `ext r` that maps `γ , v` to `δ , v`.

  <a id="23425" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23427" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23428" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="23430" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23286" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="23439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23392" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23394" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="23442" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="23465" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
  <a id="23498" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23400" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="23503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7504" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="23506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23396" class="Bound">v</a><a id="23507" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#8357" class="Function Operator">`⊑</a> <a id="23512" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="23514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23412" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="23516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7504" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="23519" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23396" class="Bound">v</a><a id="23520" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23522" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="23524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="23528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23428" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="23529" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="23531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23379" class="Function">ext-nth</a> <a id="23539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23539" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="23541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23541" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="23544" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="23546" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a>
<a id="23554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23379" class="Function">ext-nth</a> <a id="23562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23562" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="23564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23564" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="23567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="23570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23570" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23571" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23573" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23564" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="23578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23570" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We proceed by cases on the de Bruijn index `n`.

* If it is `Z`, then we just need to show that `v ≡ v`, which we have by `refl`.

* If it is `S n'`, then the goal simplifies to `nth n' γ ≡ nth (ρ n') δ`,
  which is an instance of the premise.

Now for the renaming lemma. Suppose we have a renaming that maps
variables in `γ` into variables with the same values in `δ`.  If `M`
results in `v` when evaluated in environment `γ`, then applying the
renaming to `M` produces a program that results in the same value `v` when
evaluated in `δ`.

   <a id="24597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10341" class="InductiveConstructor">⊔-intro</a> <a id="24605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24146" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24572" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24574" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24586" class="Bound">d</a><a id="24624" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24146" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24572" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24574" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24588" class="Bound">d₁</a><a id="24646" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="24648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24146" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24660" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24662" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="24672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24672" class="Bound">lt′</a><a id="24675" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24677" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="24682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="24686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24146" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24660" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24662" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24704" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">d</a><a id="24705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#24672" class="Bound">lt′</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof is by induction on the semantics of `M`.  As you can see, all
of the cases are trivial except the cases for variables and lambda.

* For a variable `x`, we make use of the premise to
  show that `nth x γ ≡ nth (ρ x) δ`.

* For a lambda abstraction, the induction hypothesis requires us to
  extend the renaming. We do so, and use the `ext-nth` lemma to show
  that the extended renaming maps variables to ones with equivalent
  values.


## Identity renamings and environment strengthening

We shall need a corollary of the renaming lemma that says that if `M`
results in `v`, then we can replace a value in the environment with a
larger one (a stronger one), and `M` still results in `v`. In particular,
if `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` and `γ ⊑ δ`, then `δ ⊢ M ↓ v`.  What does this have to do
with renaming?  It's renaming with the identity function.

The next lemma shows that renaming with an identity function is indeed
an identity function on terms. In the case of lambda abstraction, the
identity function gets extended, becoming another identity function,
but not the same one (Agda lacks extensionality).  To work around this
issue, we parameterize the proof over any function that is an
identity.

[JGS: todo: use extensionality]

<a id="26417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26101" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="26427" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26428" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="26430" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26432" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="26434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="26436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26436" class="Bound">M</a><a id="26437" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26439" class="Bound">eq</a> <a id="26442" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26444" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="26450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="26454" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26101" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="26465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26439" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="26467" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26101" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="26480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26439" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="26482" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The identity function on variables, `var-id`, is an identity function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="var-id"></a><a id="26581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26581" class="Function">var-id</a> <a id="26588" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26590" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26593" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26595" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26596" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26598" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26593" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26603" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="26605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26595" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26606" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26608" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26593" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="26615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26595" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26616" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="26618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26581" class="Function">var-id</a> <a id="26625" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26626" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26627" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26629" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26631" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26629" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="var-id-id"></a><a id="26636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26636" class="Function">var-id-id</a> <a id="26646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26648" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26650" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26651" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26652" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26654" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#25970" class="Function">is-identity</a> <a id="26668" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26651" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26670" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26581" class="Function">var-id</a>
<a id="26679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26636" class="Function">var-id-id</a> <a id="26689" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26691" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We can now prove environment strengthening by applying the renaming
lemma with the identity renaming, which gives us
`δ ⊢ rename var-id M ↓ v`, and then we apply the `rename-id` lemma
to obtain `δ ⊢ M ↓ v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Env⊑"></a><a id="26929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26929" class="Function">Env⊑</a> <a id="26934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26936" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26938" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26939" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26942" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26943" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="26945" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="26951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26939" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26952" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26954" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26955" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="26957" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="26963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26939" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26964" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26966" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26967" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26969" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#26969" class="Bound">v</a><a id="26970" class="Symbol">}</a>

In the proof that substitution reflects denotations, in the case for
lambda abstraction, we use a minor variation of `Env⊑`, in which just
the last element of the environment gets larger.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="up-env"></a><a id="27363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27363" class="Function">up-env</a> <a id="27370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27372" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27374" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27375" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="27376" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27379" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="27381" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="27387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27375" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="27388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27390" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27391" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27391" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27393" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27393" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="27395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27395" class="Bound">u₁</a> <a id="27398" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27398" class="Bound">u₂</a><a id="27400" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="27404" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27407" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27379" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="27409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7504" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="27412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27395" class="Bound">u₁</a><a id="27414" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="27418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27391" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Datatype Operator">↓</a> <a id="27422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27393" class="Bound">v</a>

class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="27562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27537" class="Bound">u₁</a><a id="27564" class="Symbol">)</a> <a site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27535" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="27572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7504" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="27575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27540" class="Bound">u₂</a><a id="27577" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="27581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27523" class="Function">nth-le</a> <a id="27588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27588" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="27591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="27593" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27588" class="Bound">lt</a>
  <a id="27600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27523" class="Function">nth-le</a> <a id="27607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27607" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="27610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="27613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#27613" class="Bound">n</a><a id="27614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27616" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#5638" class="Function">Refl⊑</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Inversion of the less-than relation for functions

What can we deduce from knowing that a function `v ↦ w` is less than
some value `u`?  What can we deduce about `u`? The answer to this
question is called the inversion property of less-than for functions.
This question is not easy to answer because of the `Dist⊑` rule, which
relates a function on the left to a pair of functions on the right.
So `u` may include several functions that, as a group, relate to
`v ↦ w`. Furthermore, because of the rules `ConjR1⊑` and `ConjR2⊑`,
there may be other values inside `u`, such as `⊥`, that have nothing
to do with `v ↦ w`. But in general, we can deduce that `u` includes
a collection of functions where the join of their domains is less
than `v` and the join of their codomains is greater than `w`.

To precisely state and prove this inversion property, we need to
define what it means for a value to _include_ a collection of values.
We also need to define how to compute the join of their domains and
codomains.


### Value membership and inclusion

Recall that we think of a value as a set of entries with the join
operator `v ⊔ w` acting like set union. The function value `v ↦ w` and
bottom value `⊥` constitute the two kinds of elements of the set.  (In
other contexts one can instead think of `⊥` as the empty set, but here
we must think of it as an element.)  We write `u ∈ v` to say that `u` is
an element of `v`, as defined below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29089" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="29095" class="Number">5</a> <a id="29097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a>

<a id="_∈_"></a><a id="29102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="29106" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="29114" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="29122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29124" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="29128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29128" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29130" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a> <a id="29134" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29128" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29138" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="29140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="29142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29142" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29146" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="29150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29150" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="29152" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29142" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29156" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="29158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29146" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="29162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29150" class="Bound">w</a>
<a id="29164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29164" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29168" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29169" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="29173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29173" class="Bound">w</a><a id="29174" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29176" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29164" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29169" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29184" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="29186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29164" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29173" class="Bound">w</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

So we can represent a collection of values simply as a value.  We
write `v ⊆ w` to say that all the elements of `v` are also in `w`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29351" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="29357" class="Number">5</a> <a id="29359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a>

<a id="_⊆_"></a><a id="29364" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a> <a id="29368" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="29376" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="29384" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29386" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="29390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29390" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="29394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29394" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="29396" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29398" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="29400" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29400" class="Bound">u</a><a id="29401" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29403" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29400" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29407" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29390" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29411" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29400" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="29417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29394" class="Bound">w</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The notions of membership and inclusion for values are closely related
to the less-than relation. They are narrower relations in that they
imply the less-than relation but not the other way around.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="∈→⊑"></a><a id="29643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29643" class="Function">∈→⊑</a> <a id="29647" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29649" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="29651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29651" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29653" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="29655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="29662" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="29692" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29651" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="29696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="29698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29653" class="Bound">v</a>
