%}#30052" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="30054" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30008" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="30058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30059" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="30064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30052" class="Bound">z</a><a id="30065" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We shall also need some inversion principles for value inclusion.  If
the union of `u` and `v` is included in `w`, then of course both `u` and
`v` are each included in `w`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊔⊆-inv"></a><a id="30268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30268" class="Function">⊔⊆-inv</a> <a id="30275" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30277" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="30279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30279" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="30281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30281" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30283" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="30285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="30292" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="30301" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30303" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30279" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="30306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="30308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30281" class="Bound">v</a><a id="30309" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="30313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30283" class="Bound">w</a>
         <a id="30324" class="Comment">---------------</a>
       <a id="30347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30279" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="30351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="30353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30283" class="Bound">w</a>  <a id="30356" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="30359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30281" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="30363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30283" class="Bound">w</a>
<a id="30365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30268" class="Function">⊔⊆-inv</a> <a id="30372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30372" class="Bound">uvw</a> <a id="30376" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="30378" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="30380" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30383" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30385" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30372" class="Bound">uvw</a> <a id="30391" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30392" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="30397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30383" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30398" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30401" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="30403" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30406" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30408" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30372" class="Bound">uvw</a> <a id="30414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30415" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="30420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30406" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30421" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30424" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In our value representation, the function value `v ↦ w` is both an
element and also a singleton set. So if `v ↦ w` is a subset of `u`,
then `v ↦ w` must be a member of `u`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↦⊆→∈"></a><a id="30625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30625" class="Function">↦⊆→∈</a> <a id="30630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30632" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="30634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30634" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30636" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="30638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30638" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="30640" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="30647" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="30654" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30634" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="30660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30636" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="30662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="30664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30638" class="Bound">u</a>
       <a id="30673" class="Comment">---------</a>
     <a id="30688" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30634" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="30694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30636" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="30696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="30698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30638" class="Bound">u</a>
<a id="30700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30625" class="Function">↦⊆→∈</a> <a id="30705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30705" class="Bound">incl</a> <a id="30710" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="30712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#30705" class="Bound">incl</a> <a id="30717" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Function values

To identify collections of functions, we define the following two
predicates. We write `Fun u` if `u` is a function value, that is, if
`u ≡ v ↦ w` for some values `v` and `w`. We write `Funs v` if all the elements
of `v` are functions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31007" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Fun"></a><a id="31012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31012" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="31016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="31024" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31026" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="31030" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Fun.fun"></a><a id="31038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31038" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="31042" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31044" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="31046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31046" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="31048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31048" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31050" class="Bound">w</a><a id="31051" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31053" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31046" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="31057" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="31059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31048" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="31064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31050" class="Bound">w</a><a id="31065" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31067" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31012" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="31073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31046" class="Bound">u</a>

<a id="Funs"></a><a id="31076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31076" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="31081" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="31089" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31091" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="31095" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31076" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="31100" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31100" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31102" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31104" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="31106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31106" class="Bound">u</a><a id="31107" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31109" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31106" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="31113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="31115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31100" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31117" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31012" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="31123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31106" class="Bound">u</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The value `⊥` is not a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="¬Fun⊥"></a><a id="31184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31184" class="Function">¬Fun⊥</a> <a id="31190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31192" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="31194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31012" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="31199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a><a id="31200" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="31202" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31184" class="Function">¬Fun⊥</a> <a id="31208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31038" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="31213" class="Symbol">())</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In our values-as-sets representation, our sets always include at least
one element. Thus, if all the elements are functions, there is at
least one that is a function.

### Domains and codomains

Returning to our goal, the inversion principle for less-than a
function, we want to show that `v ↦ w ⊑ u` implies that `u` includes
a set of function values such that the join of their domains is less
than `v` and the join of their codomains is greater than `w`.

To this end we define the following dom and cod functions.  Given some
value `u` (that represents a set of entries), `dom u` returns the join of
their domains and `cod u` returns the join of their codomains.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="dom"></a><a id="32192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32192" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="32196" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32199" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="32201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="32208" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32210" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a>

We need just one property each for `dom` and `cod`.  Given a collection of
functions represented by value `u`, and an entry `v ↦ w ∈ u`, we know
that `v` is included in the domain of `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↦∈→⊆dom"></a><a id="32573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32573" class="Function">↦∈→⊆dom</a> <a id="32581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32583" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="32585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32585" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="32587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32587" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="32589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32589" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="32591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="32598" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="32610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31076" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="32617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32585" class="Bound">u</a>  <a id="32620" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="32623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32587" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="32626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="32628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32589" class="Bound">w</a><a id="32629" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="32633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32585" class="Bound">u</a>
            <a id="32647" class="Comment">----------------------</a>
          <a id="32680" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32587" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="32684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="32686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32192" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="32690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32585" class="Bound">u</a>

   <a id="32946" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="32951" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32952" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32900" class="Bound">ih</a> <a id="32955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32887" class="Bound">u∈v</a><a id="32958" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Regarding `cod`, suppose we have a collection of functions represented
by `u`, but all of them are just copies of `v ↦ w`.  Then the `cod u` is
included in `w`.

%}</pre>

With the `dom` and `cod` functions in hand, we can make precise the
conclusion of the inversion principle for functions, which we package
into the following predicate named `factor`. We say that `v ↦ w`
_factors_ `u` into `u'` if `u'` is a included in `u`, if `u'` contains only
functions, its domain is less than `v`, and its codomain is greater
than `w`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="factor"></a><a id="33844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33844" class="Function">factor</a> <a id="33851" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33853" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33854" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="33856" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33863" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33865" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33868" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="33871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33878" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33880" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33883" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33883" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="33885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33892" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33894" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33896" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33897" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="33899" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33906" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33908" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33910" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="33914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33844" class="Function">factor</a> <a id="33921" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="33923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33923" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="33926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33926" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="33928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="33937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33923" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="33940" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33923" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="33945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="33947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="33949" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32192" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="33955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33923" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="33958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="33960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33926" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="33962" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33928" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="33966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="33968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32276" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="33972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33923" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove the inversion principle for functions by induction on the
derivation of the less-than relation. To make the induction hypothesis
stronger, we broaden the premise to `u₁ ⊑ u₂` (instead of `v ↦ w ⊑
u`), and strengthen the conclusion to say that for _every_ function
value `v ↦ w ∈ u₁`, we have that `v ↦ w` factors `u₂` into some
value `u₃`.

### Inversion of less-than for functions, the case for Trans⊑

The crux of the proof is the case for `Trans⊑`.

    u₁ ⊑ u   u ⊑ u₂
    --------------- (Trans⊑)
        u₁ ⊑ u₂

By the induction hypothesis for `u₁ ⊑ u`, we know
that `v ↦ w factors u into u'`, for some value `u'`,
so we have `Funs u'` and `u' ⊆ u`.
By the induction hypothesis for `u ⊑ u₂`, we know
that for any `v' ↦ w' ∈ u`, `v' ↦ w'` factors `u₂` into `u₃`.
With these facts in hand, we proceed by induction on `u'`
to prove that `(dom u') ↦ (cod u')` factors `u₂` into `u₃`.
We discuss each case of the proof in the text below.

    <a id="35839" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="35845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35845" class="Function">fu₂&#39;</a> <a id="35850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35852" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35853" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35856" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="35863" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35865" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35853" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35591" class="Bound">u₃₁</a> <a id="35876" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="35878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35853" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35883" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35658" class="Bound">u₃₂</a> <a id="35887" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31012" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="35893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35853" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>
          <a id="35906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35845" class="Function">fu₂&#39;</a> <a id="35911" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35912" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="35914" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35917" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="35922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35922" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35923" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35925" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35599" class="Bound">fu21&#39;</a> <a id="35933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35922" class="Bound">x</a>
          <a id="35945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35845" class="Function">fu₂&#39;</a> <a id="35950" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35951" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="35953" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35956" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="35961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35961" class="Bound">y</a><a id="35962" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35964" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35666" class="Bound">fu22&#39;</a> <a id="35972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35961" class="Bound">y</a>
          <a id="35984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35984" class="Function">u₂&#39;⊆u₂</a> <a id="35991" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35994" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35996" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="36003" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36005" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35994" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="36009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="36011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35591" class="Bound">u₃₁</a> <a id="36015" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="36017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35994" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="36019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="36021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35658" class="Bound">u₃₂</a> <a id="36025" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35994" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="36029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29102" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="36031" class="Bound">u₂</a>
          <a id="36044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35984" class="Function">u₂&#39;⊆u₂</a> <a id="36051" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36052" class="Bound">C</a><a id="36053" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36056" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="36061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36061" class="Bound">x</a><a id="36062" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35609" class="Bound">u₃₁⊆u₂</a> <a id="36073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36061" class="Bound">x</a>
          <a id="36085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35984" class="Function">u₂&#39;⊆u₂</a> <a id="36092" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36093" class="Bound">C</a><a id="36094" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36096" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36097" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="36102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36102" class="Bound">y</a><a id="36103" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36105" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#35676" class="Bound">u₃₂⊆u₂</a> <a id="36114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#36102" class="Bound">y</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Suppose `u' ≡ ⊥`. Then we have a contradiction because
  it is not the case that `Fun ⊥`.

* Suppose `u' ≡ u₁' ↦ u₂'`. Then `u₁' ↦ u₂' ∈ u` and we can apply the
  premise (the induction hypothesis from `u ⊑ u₂`) to obtain that
  `u₁' ↦ u₂'` factors of `u₂ into u₂'`. This case is complete because
  `dom u' ≡ u₁'` and `cod u' ≡ u₂'`.
  
* Suppose `u' ≡ u₁' ⊔ u₂'`. Then we have `u₁' ⊆ u` and `u₂' ⊆ u`. We also  
  have `Funs u₁'` and `Funs u₂'`, so we can apply the induction hypothesis
  for both `u₁'` and `u₂'`. So there exists values `u₃₁` and `u₃₂` such that
  `(dom u₁') ↦ (cod u₁')` factors `u` into `u₃₁` and
  `(dom u₂') ↦ (cod u₂')` factors `u` into `u₃₂`.
  We will show that `(dom u) ↦ (cod u)` factors `u` into `u₃₁ ⊔ u₃₂`.
  So we need to show that
  
        dom (u₃₁ ⊔ u₃₂) ⊑ dom (u₁' ⊔ u₂')
        cod (u₁' ⊔ u₂') ⊑ cod (u₃₁ ⊔ u₃₂)
  
  But those both follow directly from the factoring of
  `u` into `u₃₁` and `u₃₂`, using the monotonicity of `⊔` with respect to `⊑`.
  

### Inversion of less-than for functions

We come to the proof of the main lemma concerning the inversion of
less-than for functions. We show that if `u₁ ⊑ u₂`, then for any
`v ↦ w ∈ u₁`, we can factor `u₂` into `u₃` according to `v ↦ w`. We proceed
by induction on the derivation of `u₁ ⊑ u₂`, and describe each case in
the text after the Agda proof.

        <a id="37619" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37621" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="37624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37624" class="Bound">u₃</a> <a id="37627" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="37629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="37635" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="37637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#33844" class="Function">factor</a> <a id="37644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37503" class="Bound">u₂</a> <a id="37647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37624" class="Bound">u₃</a> <a id="37650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37545" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="37652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37547" class="Bound">w</a>

<a id="37687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#37488" class="Function">sub-inv</a> <a id="37695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="37696" href="{% endraw %}{{ %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="38932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="38934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38909" class="Bound">u₂₃</a><a id="38937" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{%     <a id="38949" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38950" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="38951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="DottedPattern Bound">u₂₁</a><a id="38954" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38956" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38957" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.(</a><a id="38959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38903" class="DottedPattern Bound">u₂₂</a> <a id="38963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="DottedPattern InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="38965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38909" class="DottedPattern Bound">u₂₃</a><a id="38968" class="DottedPattern Symbol">)</a><a id="38969" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38971" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="38976" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="38982" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="38984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link   <a id="39059" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="39065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39065" class="Function">f</a> <a id="39067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31076" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="39074" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39075" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="39081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38903" class="Bound">u₂₂</a> <a id="39085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="39087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="39093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38909" class="Bound">u₂₃</a><a id="39096" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="39106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39065" class="Function">f</a> <a id="39108" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39109" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="39114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39114" class="Bound">x</a><a id="39115" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39117" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31038" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="39123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39114" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="39133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39065" class="Function">f</a> <a id="39135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39136" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="39141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39141" class="Bound">y</a><a id="39142" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39144" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31038" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="39150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39141" class="Bound">y</a>
        <a id="39160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39160" class="Function">g</a> <a id="39162" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39164" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="39183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38909" class="Bound">u₂₃</a><a id="39186" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#29364" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="39190" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39191" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="39197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38903" %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38896" class="Bound">u₂₁</a> <a id="39207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="39209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#38909" class="Bound">u₂₃</a><a id="39212" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="39222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39160" class="Function">g</a> <a id="39224" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39225" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="39230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39230" class="Bound">x</a><a id="39231" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39233" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39235" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="39240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39230" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="39250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39160" class="Function">g</a> <a id="39252" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39253" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="39258" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39258" class="Bound">y</a><a id="39259" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39261" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39263" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="39268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#39258" class="Bound">y</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let `v` and `w` be arbitrary values.

* Case `Bot⊑`. So `u₁ ≡ ⊥`. We have `v ↦ w ∈ ⊥`, but that is impossible.

* Case `ConjL⊑`.

        u₁₁ ⊑ u₂   u₁₂ ⊑ u₂
        -------------------
        u₁₁ ⊔ u₁₂ ⊑ u₂

  Given that `v ↦ w ∈ u₁₁ ⊔ u₁₂`, there are two subcases to consider.

  * Subcase `v ↦ w ∈ u₁₁`. We conclude by the induction
    hypothesis for `u₁₁ ⊑ u₂`.
  
  * Subcase `v ↦ w ∈ u₁₂`. We conclude by the induction hypothesis
    for `u₁₂ ⊑ u₂`.

* Case `ConjR1⊑`.

        u₁ ⊑ u₂₁
        --------------
        u₁ ⊑ u₂₁ ⊔ u₂₂

  Given that `v ↦ w ∈ u₁`, the induction hypothesis for `u₁ ⊑ u₂₁`
  gives us that `v ↦ w` factors `u₂₁` into `u₃₁` for some `u₃₁`.
  To show that `v ↦ w` also factors `u₂₁ ⊔ u₂₂` into `u₃₁`,
  we just need to show that `u₃₁ ⊆ u₂₁ ⊔ u₂₂`, but that follows
  directly from `u₃₁ ⊆ u₂₁`.

* Case `ConjR2⊑`. This case follows by reasoning similar to
  the case for `ConjR1⊑`.

* Case `Trans⊑`. 

        u₁ ⊑ u   u ⊑ u₂
        ---------------
            u₁ ⊑ u₂
        
  By the induction hypothesis for `u₁ ⊑ u`, we know
  that `v ↦ w` factors `u` into `u'`, for some value `u'`,
  so we have `Funs u'` and `u' ⊆ u`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `u ⊑ u₂`, we know
  that for any `v' ↦ w' ∈ u`, `v' ↦ w'` factors `u₂`.
  Now we apply the lemma sub-inv-trans, which gives us
  some `u₃` such that `(dom u') ↦ (cod u')` factors `u₂` into `u₃`.
  We show that `v ↦ w` also factors `u₂` into `u₃`.
  From `dom u₃ ⊑ dom u'` and `dom u' ⊑ v`, we have `dom u₃ ⊑ v`.
  From `w ⊑ cod u'` and `cod u' ⊑ cod u₃`, we have `w ⊑ cod u₃`,
  and this case is complete.

* Case `Fun⊑`.

        u₂₁ ⊑ u₁₁  u₁₂ ⊑ u₂₂
        ---------------------
        u₁₁ ↦ u₁₂ ⊑ u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂

  Given that `v ↦ w ∈ u₁₁ ↦ u₁₂`, we have `v ≡ u₁₁` and `w ≡ u₁₂`.
  We show that `u₁₁ ↦ u₁₂` factors `u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂` into itself.
  We need to show that `dom (u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂) ⊑ u₁₁` and `u₁₂ ⊑ cod (u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂)`,
  but that is equivalent to our premises `u₂₁ ⊑ u₁₁` and `u₁₂ ⊑ u₂₂`.

* Case `Dist⊑`.

        ---------------------------------------------
        u₂₁ ↦ (u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃) ⊑ (u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂) ⊔ (u₂₁ ↦ u₂₃)

  Given that `v ↦ w ∈ u₂₁ ↦ (u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃)`, we have `v ≡ u₂₁`
  and `w ≡ u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃`.
  We show that `u₂₁ ↦ (u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃)` factors `(u₂₁ ↦ u₂₂) ⊔ (u₂₁ ↦ u₂₃)`
  into itself. We have `u₂₁ ⊔ u₂₁ ⊑ u₂₁`, and also
  `u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃ ⊑ u₂₂ ⊔ u₂₃`, so the proof is complete.


We conclude this section with two corollaries of the sub-inv lemma.
First, we have the following property that is convenient to use in
later proofs. We specialize the premise to just `v ↦ w ⊑ u₁`
and we modify the conclusion to say that for every
`v' ↦ w' ∈ u₂`, we have `v' ⊑ v`.

The second corollary is the inversion rule that one would expect for
less-than with functions on the left and right-hand sides.

## Notes

The denotational semantics presented in this chapter is an example of
a _filter model_ (Barendregt, Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, 1983). Filter
models use type systems with intersection types to precisely
characterize runtime behavior (Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, and Salle,
1979). The notation that we use in this chapter is not that of type
systems and intersection types, but the `Value` data type is isomorphic
to types (`↦` is `→`, `⊔` is `∧`, `⊥` is `⊤`), the `⊑` relation is the
inverse of subtyping `<:`, and the evaluation relation `ρ ⊢ M ↓ v` is
isomorphic to a type system. Write `Γ` instead of `ρ`, `A` instead of `v`, and
replace `↓` with `:` and one has a typing judgement `Γ ⊢ M : A`.
By varying the definition of subtyping and using different choices of
type atoms, intersection type systems provide semantics for many different
untyped λ calculi, from full beta to the lazy and call-by-value calculi
(Alessi, Barbanera, and Dezani-Ciancaglini, 2006) (Rocca and Paolini, 2004).
The denotational semantics in this chapter corresponds to the BCD
system (Barendregt, Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, 1983).  Part 3 of the
book _Lambda Calculus with Types_ describes a framework for
intersection type systems that enables results similar to the ones in
this chapter, but for the entire family of intersection type systems
(Barendregt, Dekkers, and Statman, 2013).

The two ideas of using finite tables to represent functions and of
relaxing table lookup to enable self application first appeared in a
technical report by Gordon Plotkin (1972) and are later described in
an article in Theoretical Computer Science (Plotkin 1993).  In that
work, the inductive definition of `Value` is a bit different than the
one we use:
 
    Value = C + ℘f(Value) × ℘f(Value)
 
where `C` is a set of constants and `℘f` means finite powerset.  The pairs
in `℘f(Value) × ℘f(Value)` represent input-output mappings, just as in
this chapter. The finite powersets are used to enable a function table
to appear in the input and in the output. These differences amount to
changing where the recursion appears in the definition of `Value`.
Plotkin's model is an example of a _graph model_ of the untyped lambda
calculus (Barendregt, 1984). In a graph model, the semantics is
presented as a function from programs and environments to (possibly
infinite) sets of values. The semantics in this chapter is instead
defined as a relation, but set-valued functions are isomorphic to
relations. We choose to present the semantics as a relation because
the functional approach requires a kind of existential quantifier that
is not present in Agda.

[PLW: What kind of existential is required?]

Dana Scott's ℘(ω) (1976) and Engeler's B(A) (1981) are two more
examples of graph models. Both use the following inductive definition
of `Value`.
 
    Value = C + ℘f(Value) × Value
 
The use of `Value` instead of `℘f(Value)` in the output does not restrict
expressiveness compared to Plotkin's model because the semantics use
sets of values and a pair of sets `(V, V')` can be represented as a set
of pairs `{ (V, v') | v' ∈ V' }`.  In Scott's ℘(ω), the above values are
mapped to and from the natural numbers using a kind of Godel encoding.
